        - The car's lateral deviation from the racing line is given by the d-coordinate: [0.1, 0.05, 0.0, -0.05, -0.1, -0.15, -0.1, -0.05, 0.0, 0.05, 0.1]

        
        - The car's speed along the racing line is given by the s-speed: [5.5, 5.6, 5.5, 5.7, 5.6, 5.5, 5.6, 5.5, 5.7, 5.6, 5.5]

        
        - The car's speed perpendicular to the racing line is given by the d-speed: [0.0, 0.05, 0.0, -0.05, 0.0, 0.05, 0.0, -0.05, 0.0, 0.05, 0.0]

        
        - The distance to the left wall is: [1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5]


        - The distance to the right wall is: [1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5, 1.5]

 
        - Bool if the car is reversing: False

          
        - Bool if the car has crashed: False

        
        - Bool if the car is facing the wall: False


   
        Use these guides to reason:

Oscillations in d-coordinate under 0.3m or d-speed under 0.5m/s are negligible.
Hint 7:
